/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;

CREATE TABLE `Resources` (
  `res_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `res_lan` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_title` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_type` varchar(10) NOT NULL,
  `res_subtype` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_format` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_difficulty` smallint(6) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_duration` double DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_privilege` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_usr_id_owner` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_tpl_name` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_res_id_root` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_mod_res_id_test` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_status` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_create_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_upd_user` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_upd_date` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_src_type` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_src_link` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_code` varchar(30) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_instructor_name` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_instructor_organization` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_annotation` text,
  `res_long_desc` longtext,
  `res_desc` text,
  `res_sco_version` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_vod_duration` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_img_link` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_vod_main` longtext,
  `res_scor_identifier` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `res_first_res_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`res_id`),
  KEY `IX_resources_first_res_id` (`res_first_res_id`),
  KEY `IX_RESOURCES_RES_STATUS` (`res_id`,`res_status`),
  KEY `IX_RESOURCES_RES_TEST` (`res_mod_res_id_test`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

--
-- Table structure for table `TrackingHistory`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `TrackingHistory`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `TrackingHistory` (
  `tkh_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `tkh_type` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `tkh_usr_ent_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `tkh_cos_res_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `tkh_create_timestamp` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`tkh_id`),
  KEY `IX_TRACKINGHISTORY` (`tkh_type`,`tkh_usr_ent_id`,`tkh_cos_res_id`),
  KEY `IX_TRACKINGHISTORY_COS_RES_ID` (`tkh_cos_res_id`),
  KEY `IX_TRACKINGHISTORY_USR_ENT_ID` (`tkh_usr_ent_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

--
-- Dumping data for table `TrackingHistory`
--

LOCK TABLES `TrackingHistory` WRITE;
/*!40000 ALTER TABLE `TrackingHistory` DISABLE KEYS */;
/*!40000 ALTER TABLE `TrackingHistory` ENABLE KEYS */;
UNLOCK TABLES;

--
-- Table structure for table `UploadLog`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `UploadLog`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `UploadLog` (
  `ulg_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ulg_type` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `ulg_subtype` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `ulg_usr_id_owner` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `ulg_file_name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `ulg_status` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `ulg_create_datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `ulg_upd_datetime` datetime NOT NULL,
  `ulg_desc` longtext,
  `ulg_process` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `ulg_method` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ulg_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

--
-- Table structure for table `UserClassification`
--

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `UserClassification`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `UserClassification` (

  `tnd_on_itm_cnt` int(11) NOT NULL,

  `tnd_link_tnd_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_itm_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,

  `tnd_create_usr_id` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `tnd_upd_timestamp` datetime NOT NULL,
  `tnd_upd_usr_id` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `tnd_ext1` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_ext2` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_ext3` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_ext4` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_ext5` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_desc` text,
  `tnd_order` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_owner_ent_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `tnd_code` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `tnd_syn_timestamp` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`tnd_id`),
  KEY `IX_AETREENODE_CAT_ID` (`tnd_cat_id`),

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `SP_getCMTAndOfflineRs` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_AUTO_CREATE_USER,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `SP_getCMTAndOfflineRs`(IN `tkh_id` int,IN `ccr_id` int)
BEGIN

   select cmt_is_contri_by_score,cmt_id,cmt_title,cmt_max_score,cmt_contri_rate,cmt_pass_score,cmt_duration, cmt_place,
   cmt_status,cmt_status_desc_option,mtv_status,mtv_score,res_status,res_id,res_title,res_subtype,mov_status,
   cmr_ccr_id ,cmr_id,cmr_contri_rate, cmr_status,cmr_status_desc_option,res_id,res_type,res_title,res_status,res_subtype,
	 res_desc,mod_max_score,mod_pass_score,mov_score,mov_status,mov_tkh_id 
   From CourseMeasurement  
   left join (  select cmr_ccr_id ,cmr_id,cmr_contri_rate, cmr_status,cmr_status_desc_option,res_id,res_type,res_title,res_status,res_subtype, 
             res_desc,mod_max_score,mod_pass_score,mov_score,mov_status,mov_tkh_id 
              From CourseModuleCriteria, Resources, Module 
                 left join ModuleEvaluation on (mov_mod_id = mod_res_id and mov_tkh_id = tkh_id ) 
                  where cmr_del_timestamp is null    and cmr_res_id = res_id and res_id = mod_res_id   )
   cmr on (cmt_cmr_id = cmr.cmr_id) left join measurementEvaluation on (cmt_id = mtv_cmt_id and mtv_tkh_id = tkh_id) 
  where cmt_delete_timestamp is null and cmt_ccr_id = @ccr_id ;

END ;;
DELIMITER ;

/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `sp_get_top_level_group_id` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_AUTO_CREATE_USER,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `sp_get_top_level_group_id`(IN `usr_ent_id` int)
BEGIN
	 select distinct tce_ent_id 
	 From tcTrainingCenterOfficer,
				tcTrainingCenterTargetEntity  tp,
				tcTrainingCenter,
	      Entity
	 where tco_usr_ent_id = @usr_ent_id and tco_tcr_id = tcr_id 
	  and tcr_status = 'OK' and tce_tcr_id = tcr_id 
		and tce_ent_id = ent_id and ent_delete_usr_id IS NULL and ent_delete_timestamp IS NULL
	  and not exists(
	     select ern_child_ent_id from EntityRelation tem 
			 where ern_type = 'USG_PARENT_USG' and
	     tp.tce_ent_id= tem.ern_child_ent_id and 
	     exists(
				 select distinct ern_child_ent_id From tcTrainingCenterOfficer,
				 tcTrainingCenterTargetEntity,
				 tcTrainingCenter,
				 Entity,
				 EntityRelation ern
				 where tco_usr_ent_id = usr_ent_id and tco_tcr_id = tcr_id 
					and tcr_status = 'OK'
					and tce_tcr_id = tcr_id 
					and tce_ent_id = ern_child_ent_id 
					and tce_ent_id = ent_id and ent_delete_usr_id IS NULL and ent_delete_timestamp IS NULL
					and tem.ern_ancestor_ent_id = ern.ern_child_ent_id
	     )
	);

END ;;
